Statement 3 is incorrect. The Climate and Clean Air Coalition (CCAC) is a very important partnership initiative, and the UNEP is a key partner and plays a leading role in its activities.  The CCAC is not independent of the UNEP; it's a collaborative effort involving many international organizations, governments, and the private sector, with the UNEP's strong involvement.


**3. With reference to India's engagement with international environmental agreements, consider the following statements:**

1. India was a signatory to the New York Declaration on Forests from its inception.
2. India's participation in CITES (Convention on International Trade in Endangered Species) involves the regulation of domestic trade in endangered species solely through CITES provisions.
3.  India's national laws, such as the Wildlife Protection Act, are not integrated with its international commitments under CITES.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 2 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. India was indeed a signatory to the New York Declaration on Forests from its inception.  Its participation demonstrates its commitment to international efforts for forest conservation.

Statement 2 is incorrect. While India's participation in CITES is crucial, the regulation of domestic trade in endangered species isn't solely based on CITES provisions.  India has its own domestic laws and regulations, primarily the Wildlife Protection Act of 1972, which plays a significant role in controlling the trade and protection of endangered species within the country.  CITES provides the international framework, but domestic laws are essential for implementation.

Statement 3 is incorrect. India's national laws, particularly the Wildlife Protection Act of 1972, are explicitly integrated with its international commitments under CITES.  The Act's schedules and provisions align with CITES appendices, ensuring that India's domestic regulations are consistent with its international obligations.  The integration is vital for effective enforcement and conservation efforts.



**4. With reference to the  Hyderabad's urban forestry, consider the following statements:**

1.  Hyderabad's recognition as a "Tree City of the World" was solely based on its commitment to growing urban forests in a single year.
2. The UN-Habitat played a significant role in assessing and recognizing Hyderabad's urban forestry achievements.
3.  Hyderabad's successful urban forestry initiatives are entirely independent of any international collaborations or funding.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) None
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. The recognition of Hyderabad as a Tree City of the World wasn't based solely on a single year's commitment.  It was a result of sustained efforts and ongoing commitment to urban forestry, demonstrating a long-term dedication to greening the city.  The assessment considers multiple years of data and progress.

Statement 2 is incorrect. While UN agencies such as the UN-Habitat often support urban forestry initiatives globally, the specific recognition in this case was by the United Nations Capital Development Fund (UNCDF) and the Arbor Day Foundation, not UN-Habitat directly.  Different organizations have different programs for recognizing achievements in urban greening.

Statement 3 is incorrect. Hyderabad's urban forestry achievements are unlikely to be entirely independent of international collaborations or funding.  Many urban development projects, including those related to greening initiatives, often involve collaboration and partnerships with international organizations or receive funding from various sources.  Such collaborations can provide expertise, resources, and support for successful implementation.

Here are some UPSC-style multiple choice questions based on the provided target content, adhering to all specified instructions.  Each question is designed to be challenging and incorporates plausible distractors.


**1. Consider the following statements:**

1.  The Asaf Jahi Nizams implemented a system of revenue administration in Hyderabad based on the ancient Chola system of land measurement.
2.  The subsidiary alliance, a key feature of British foreign policy, was initially applied to Hyderabad during the reign of Aurangzeb.
3.  Kondapur, a significant urban center near Hyderabad, played a crucial role in the Deccan's early trade networks during the Mughal period.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. While the Asaf Jahi Nizams ruled Hyderabad, their revenue administration system wasn't based on the Chola system. The Nizami system had its own distinct features, often influenced by Persian and other regional administrative practices.  The Chola system was primarily relevant to South India centuries earlier.

Statement 2 is incorrect. The subsidiary alliance was a British policy, not one implemented by the Mughals. Aurangzeb's reign predates the British East India Company's dominance and the widespread use of the subsidiary alliance.  The policy was primarily applied during the later stages of the Company's rule and the early British Raj.

Statement 3 is correct. Kondapur's proximity to Hyderabad and its location in the Deccan region strongly suggest its involvement in historical trade routes, particularly during the Mughal period when Hyderabad emerged as a significant trading center. Archaeological evidence and historical accounts often support the presence of robust trade networks in and around such strategically located settlements.  The statement doesn't claim a *primary* role, making it more difficult to challenge factually.


**2. With reference to Hyderabad's history and governance, consider the following statements:**

1.  Bussy, a French military commander, established a significant French military presence in Hyderabad that lasted well into the 19th century.
2.  The Indian Army's takeover of Hyderabad in 1948 was a swift and bloodless affair, facilitated by the Nizam's immediate surrender.
3.  The Hyderabad Municipal Corporation, established in the late 19th century, played a crucial role in shaping the city's urban landscape.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 3 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. While Bussy did have a significant military presence in Hyderabad, it was relatively short-lived compared to the long-term presence of the Nizams. The statement overstates the duration of French influence.

Statement 2 is incorrect. The Indian Army's intervention in Hyderabad in 1948, known as "Operation Polo," was not bloodless.  It involved military action and resulted in casualties and subsequent social and political upheaval.  The Nizam's surrender came after the military action, not before.

Statement 3 is partially correct but needs clarification. The Hyderabad Municipal Corporation's establishment date might vary depending on the specific iteration of the governing body.  However, a municipal body with a significant role in urban planning and governance existed in Hyderabad for a considerable time, impacting the city's development.  The question focuses on this role, not the exact date.


**3. With reference to the geographical features and natural resources of India, consider the following statements:**

1.  The CGWA, established under the Environment (Protection) Act, 1986, classifies over 50% of India's districts as "overexploited" or "critical" regarding groundwater resources.
2.  India's largest area under groundwater irrigation is located primarily in the Indo-Gangetic plains.
3.  The Sunderbans Tiger Reserve has the largest area designated as "Critical Tiger Habitat" among all tiger reserves in India.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. The percentage of overexploited or critically overexploited districts is significantly lower than 50%, as per CGWA data. The statement exaggerates the severity of the groundwater crisis to mislead.

Statement 2 is correct. The Indo-Gangetic plains are known for intensive agriculture and substantial reliance on groundwater irrigation.  This is a well-established geographical fact.

Statement 3 is incorrect. The Nagarjunsagar-Srisailam Tiger Reserve possesses a substantially larger core area (Critical Tiger Habitat) compared to the Sunderbans.  The question utilizes the common misconception that Sunderbans is the largest in terms of critical tiger habitat.


**4. With reference to the Wildlife Protection Act, 1972, and its implications, consider the following statements:**

1.  Schedule VI of the Wildlife Protection Act, 1972, lists only plants that are genetically modified and thus require strict regulatory control.
2.  Cultivation of any plant species listed under Schedule VI of the Wildlife Protection Act, 1972, is strictly prohibited without a license.
3.  The 1991 amendment to the Wildlife Protection Act clarified the definition of "invasive species" and included specific provisions for their management.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 2 and 3 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. Schedule VI of the Wildlife Protection Act includes a broader range of plants than just genetically modified organisms. It encompasses plants that are endangered, threatened, or considered harmful to the ecosystem, irrespective of genetic modification.

Statement 2 is correct.  Schedule VI plants require a license for cultivation, reflecting the need to protect these species from overexploitation or misuse.

Statement 3 is incorrect. While the 1991 amendment did strengthen the Act, the specific definition and management of invasive species were further refined and clarified in subsequent legislation and guidelines.  The statement oversimplifies the complexities of legal evolution.


**5. With reference to India's National Policy on Biofuels, consider the following statements:**

1.  Rotten potatoes and damaged wheat grains are explicitly excluded as raw materials for biofuel production due to their low energy content and potential for contamination.
2.  Cassava and sugar beet are among the primary sources of raw materials for biofuel production, as specified in the National Policy on Biofuels.
3.  The policy prioritizes the use of feedstocks that do not compete with food crops, such as horse grams, but allows for the use of surplus or damaged grains under specific conditions.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1, 2, and 3
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. While the policy prioritizes high-yield and suitable feedstocks, it doesn't explicitly exclude rotten potatoes or damaged wheat grains.  The use of such materials might be considered under specific circumstances and subject to technological feasibility and quality control.

Statement 2 is correct. Cassava and sugar beet are explicitly mentioned as potential feedstocks in the National Policy on Biofuels.

Statement 3 is correct.  The policy emphasizes the use of non-food crops for biofuel production to avoid competition with food security. However, it acknowledges the potential use of surplus or damaged food crops under certain conditions.  The statement accurately reflects the balance between biofuel production and food security.

**1. Consider the following statements regarding the use of raw materials in ethanol production:**

1.  Cassava is a primary raw material used in ethanol production in several regions globally, particularly in tropical and subtropical areas.
2. Damaged wheat grains, unsuitable for direct human consumption, can be utilized as a feedstock in ethanol production processes.
3.  Sugarcane bagasse, a byproduct of sugarcane processing, is a significant source of biomass for ethanol production, offering a sustainable alternative.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (a) 1 and 2 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. Cassava, a starchy root crop, is a well-established raw material for ethanol production. Its high starch content makes it suitable for fermentation processes, and its cultivation is particularly viable in regions with limited water resources.  The use of cassava contributes to diversification of ethanol sources, reducing reliance on traditional grains.

Statement 2 is also correct. Damaged wheat grains, often unfit for human consumption due to damage or spoilage, represent a significant waste stream. Their utilization in ethanol production offers a valuable method of waste management and resource recovery, transforming otherwise unusable material into a renewable fuel source.  This approach enhances resource efficiency and reduces environmental impact.

Statement 3 is incorrect. While sugarcane bagasse *can* be used in ethanol production, it is not primarily used as a direct feedstock in the same way as cassava or damaged wheat grains.  Sugarcane bagasse is a lignocellulosic biomass, requiring more complex and energy-intensive pretreatment steps before fermentation.  It's typically utilized in second-generation biofuel processes, which are still under development and not yet as widely adopted as first-generation methods using starch or sugar.  It is better to consider it as a supplementary biofuel source.



**2. With reference to Sugar beet cultivation, consider the following statements:**

1. Sugar beet is grown predominantly in tropical regions known for their high temperatures and abundant rainfall.
2. Sugar beet has a higher sugar content compared to sugarcane, making it a more efficient source of sucrose.
3.  Sugar beet is classified botanically as a root crop, with its sugar-rich taproot serving as the primary source of sugar for extraction.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 3 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) 2 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (b) 3 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. Sugar beet thrives in temperate climates with cooler temperatures and well-distributed rainfall.  Tropical regions with high temperatures and humidity are generally unsuitable for optimal sugar beet growth and sugar accumulation.  The plant's physiology is adapted to moderate conditions.

Statement 2 is incorrect. While sugar beet is a significant source of sugar, sugarcane generally boasts a higher sugar content per unit area.  The relative efficiency depends on several factors, including climate, cultivation practices, and variety.  Sugarcane's superior performance in tropical climates makes it the dominant sugar crop globally.

Statement 3 is correct. Sugar beet is a root crop, and its large, fleshy taproot stores sucrose, the primary sugar extracted for various applications, including food and biofuel production.  The taproot's structure is crucial for efficient sugar accumulation and ease of harvesting.  This contrasts with sugarcane, which is a stem-based crop.



**3. With reference to the Compensatory Afforestation Fund Management and Planning Authority (CAMPA), consider the following statements:**

1.  The CAMPA Act, 2016, mandates strict adherence to a 90:10 fund distribution ratio between state and national levels respectively, with no exceptions.
2.  People's participation in compensatory afforestation programs is legally mandated under the CAMPA Act, 2016,  requiring community involvement in all projects.
3. The CAMPA exists at both the national and state levels, facilitating the management and planning of compensatory afforestation programs across India.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 3 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) 2 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (b) 3 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. While the CAMPA Act designates a fund distribution, it's not strictly a mandatory 90:10 ratio.  The allocation can vary depending on specific project needs and approvals.  The flexibility is designed to accommodate diverse circumstances and regional variations.

Statement 2 is incorrect. The CAMPA Act encourages people’s participation, but it's not a strict legal mandate for all projects.  While community involvement is highly beneficial and often incorporated, the Act doesn't impose it as an absolute requirement for all compensatory afforestation initiatives.  The emphasis is on promoting cooperation, not rigid enforcement.

Statement 3 is correct. The CAMPA structure includes both national and state-level authorities, ensuring coordinated management and planning across India. This hierarchical system allows for centralized policy direction while also enabling adaptation to regional contexts.  The two-tiered approach is crucial for effective implementation.


**4. With reference to the Agasthyamala Biosphere Reserve, consider the following statements:**

1. The Agasthyamala Biosphere Reserve encompasses the Mudumalai, Sathyamangalam, and Wayanad Wildlife Sanctuaries.
2. The Kalakad Mundanthurai Tiger Reserve is a key component of the Agasthyamala Biosphere Reserve, contributing significantly to its biodiversity.
3. The Agasthyamala Biosphere Reserve is primarily located in the state of Karnataka, with minor portions extending into neighboring states.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 2 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (b) 2 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect.  The Mudumalai, Sathyamangalam, and Wayanad Wildlife Sanctuaries are located in a different biosphere reserve, namely the Nilgiri Biosphere Reserve.  The Agasthyamala Biosphere Reserve is geographically distinct and harbors its own unique set of protected areas.

Statement 2 is correct. The Kalakad Mundanthurai Tiger Reserve forms a vital part of the Agasthyamala Biosphere Reserve, contributing significantly to its conservation efforts.  Its inclusion reflects the importance of tiger conservation within the reserve's overall biodiversity management strategy.

Statement 3 is incorrect. The Agasthyamala Biosphere Reserve is primarily situated across the border of Kerala and Tamil Nadu, not Karnataka.  While other reserves might be in Karnataka, the core of Agasthyamala is in the southern Western Ghats region.


**5. With reference to National Parks located in the temperate alpine zone, consider the following statements:**

1. Manas National Park is entirely situated within the temperate alpine zone, characterized by high-altitude flora and fauna.
2. Valley of Flowers National Park is a prominent example of a national park located within the temperate alpine zone of the Himalayas.
3.  Neora Valley National Park, known for its diverse ecosystem, includes a significant portion within the temperate alpine zone.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 2 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (b) 2 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. Manas National Park is primarily located in the Brahmaputra valley, a lower-altitude region, and does not fall within the temperate alpine zone.  Its ecosystem is distinct from the high-altitude environments of the alpine zone.

Statement 2 is correct. The Valley of Flowers National Park is situated in the western Himalayas, specifically within the temperate alpine zone, known for its unique high-altitude meadows and diverse flora.  Its location is directly within the described geographical area.

Statement 3 is incorrect. Neora Valley National Park, while having a high-altitude component, is not primarily located in the temperate alpine zone. Its ecosystem encompasses a broader range of altitudes and vegetation types.


**6.  With reference to the Ramsar Convention and Indian Wetlands, consider the following statements:**

1.  The Ramsar Convention mandates the Government of India to protect and conserve all wetlands within its territory.
2. The Wetlands (Conservation and Management) Rules, 2010, were solely based on the recommendations of the Ramsar Convention, with no other considerations.
3. The Wetlands (Conservation and Management) Rules, 2010, explicitly encompass the drainage areas or catchment regions of designated wetlands.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 3 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) 2 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (b) 3 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. The Ramsar Convention encourages, but does not mandate, the protection of all wetlands.  It focuses on designating Wetlands of International Importance, which are then subject to specific conservation efforts.  The convention works through a system of voluntary commitments.

Statement 2 is incorrect.  While the Ramsar Convention heavily influenced the framing of the Wetlands (Conservation and Management) Rules, 2010, it wasn't the sole basis.  Indian legal frameworks and environmental considerations also played significant roles in the rule-making process.  The rules are a blend of international and national priorities.

Statement 3 is correct. The 2010 rules include the drainage areas or catchment regions, recognizing the interconnectedness of wetlands and their surrounding ecosystems.  This holistic approach is crucial for effective wetland management.  The inclusion aims to protect the entire hydrological system supporting the wetland.


**7. With reference to the National Green Tribunal (NGT) and the Central Pollution Control Board (CPCB), consider the following statements:**

1. The NGT was established through an Act of Parliament, while the CPCB was created by an executive order of the government.
2. The NGT's primary function is to provide environmental justice and reduce the burden on higher courts, while the CPCB's main focus is on promoting cleanliness of streams and wells.
3. Both NGT and CPCB are under the Ministry of Environment, Forest and Climate Change (MOEFCC).

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (c) 1 and 3 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. The NGT derives its authority from a specific Act of Parliament, granting it quasi-judicial powers. The CPCB, on the other hand, is a statutory body established under an executive order, operating under the provisions of various environmental laws.  The difference in their establishment reflects their distinct roles.

Statement 2 is partially correct in highlighting the NGT's role in environmental justice and reducing court burden. However, the CPCB's mandate is broader than just streams and wells; it includes air and water quality management across the country.  The description understates the CPCB's responsibilities.

Statement 3 is correct. Both NGT and CPCB function under the overall umbrella of the MOEFCC, ensuring coordination in environmental governance.  Their alignment within the ministry ensures streamlined policy and implementation.


**8. With reference to the Pakhui Wildlife Sanctuary, consider the following statements:**

1. Pakhui Wildlife Sanctuary is located in the state of Manipur, known for its diverse biodiversity and unique ecosystems.
2. Pakhui Wildlife Sanctuary is primarily known for its significant population of the one-horned rhinoceros, a flagship species of the region.
3.  Pakhui Wildlife Sanctuary is a crucial habitat for a variety of endangered flora and fauna, contributing to the conservation of biodiversity in Northeast India.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 3 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) 2 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (b) 3 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. Pakhui Wildlife Sanctuary is located in Arunachal Pradesh, not Manipur.  The two states are geographically distinct, with different ecological characteristics.

Statement 2 is incorrect.  While Pakhui Wildlife Sanctuary is rich in biodiversity, it's not primarily known for a significant population of one-horned rhinoceros.  That species is more strongly associated with other sanctuaries in Assam and Nepal.

Statement 3 is correct. Pakhui Wildlife Sanctuary plays a vital role in conserving the diverse flora and fauna of Arunachal Pradesh, significantly contributing to the region's biodiversity.  Its location in the Eastern Himalayas makes it a crucial habitat for numerous species.



**9. With reference to the Global Alliance for Climate-Smart Agriculture (GACSA), consider the following statements:**

1. GACSA was established primarily as an initiative of the World Bank, aiming to promote climate-resilient agricultural practices globally.
2. GACSA's activities include supporting research and development of climate-smart agricultural technologies and practices.
3. GACSA operates primarily through bilateral agreements with individual countries, focusing on specific national agricultural policies.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?


(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) 2 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (b) 2 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect.  While the World Bank is involved, GACSA is primarily promoted by the Food and Agriculture Organization of the United Nations (FAO),  a specialized agency of the UN. Its establishment reflects a broader international effort, not solely the World Bank's initiative.

Statement 2 is correct. GACSA supports research, development, and dissemination of climate-smart agricultural technologies and practices.  This is a key pillar of its efforts to enhance food security and environmental sustainability.

Statement 3 is incorrect.  GACSA operates through a more collaborative and multi-stakeholder approach, involving various international organizations, governments, and NGOs.  Its actions are not limited to bilateral agreements.  The approach is designed to create a global network of support.

Here are some UPSC-style Multiple Choice Questions (MCQs) based on the provided target content, adhering to all specified criteria.  Each question includes the correct answer and a detailed explanation.


**1. Consider the following statements about Arunachal Pradesh:**

1. The Bugun Liocichl, a bird species, is endemic to Arunachal Pradesh and was discovered in 2006.
2.  The Tawang Monastery, a significant Buddhist site, is located in the easternmost district of Arunachal Pradesh, bordering Myanmar.
3.  The percentage of Recorded Forest Areas (RFAs) to the total geographical area of Arunachal Pradesh is significantly lower than the national average.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 3 only
(c) 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (b) 1 and 3 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. The Bugun liocichla is indeed endemic to Arunachal Pradesh and its discovery is a significant event in Indian ornithology.  However, the year of discovery is mentioned incorrectly in the statement.

Statement 2 is incorrect. While the Tawang Monastery is in Arunachal Pradesh, it is not located in the easternmost district bordering Myanmar. The easternmost point of Arunachal Pradesh is Kibithu, and the monastery is situated in the Tawang district, which shares a border with Tibet/China.  The statement attempts to mislead the candidate by combining true elements (Tawang Monastery location and Arunachal Pradesh's eastern border) with a false detail (bordering Myanmar).

Statement 3 is correct. Arunachal Pradesh has a very high percentage of forest cover, but the proportion of RFAs to its total geographical area is lower than the national average. This reflects the unique land tenure systems and the relatively lower degree of formal forest management in the state compared to other parts of India.  The statement plays on the candidate's potential assumption that a high forest cover percentage automatically translates to a high RFA percentage.

Therefore, only statements 1 and 3 are correct.


**2. With reference to Arunachal Pradesh's geography and ecology, consider the following statements:**

1. The state experiences a high incidence of thunderstorms due to its location in the Himalayas and its proximity to the Bay of Bengal.
2. The Shivalik Range forms a significant part of Arunachal Pradesh's western boundary, creating a natural barrier.
3. The Subansiri River, originating in the Himalayas, flows through Arunachal Pradesh and contributes to the Brahmaputra River system.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (c) 1 and 3 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. Arunachal Pradesh's location in the Eastern Himalayas, coupled with its proximity to the Bay of Bengal, results in a high frequency of thunderstorms due to orographic rainfall and the convergence of moist air masses.

Statement 2 is incorrect. The statement is misleading. While the Shivalik Range is part of the Himalayan system, it is not a prominent feature of Arunachal Pradesh's western boundary. The state's western boundary is more complex, involving the higher Himalayan ranges.  This statement uses a true fact (Shivalik Range being part of the Himalayas) in a deceptive context to create a distractor.

Statement 3 is correct. The Subansiri River is a major river system originating in the Himalayas, flowing through Arunachal Pradesh, and ultimately joining the Brahmaputra River.  

Therefore, only statements 1 and 3 are correct.


**3. With reference to Arunachal Pradesh's socio-cultural aspects, consider the following statements:**

1. The Dree festival, a significant agricultural festival, is celebrated primarily by the Nyishi tribe.
2. The Monpa tribe, concentrated in the western districts, primarily practices Tibetan Buddhism.
3.  The state's population lacks Scheduled Castes, a unique demographic feature among Indian states.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (d) 1, 2, and 3

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. The Dree festival is a significant agricultural festival predominantly celebrated by the Nyishi tribe of Arunachal Pradesh.  This statement is a straight-forward factual recall.

Statement 2 is correct. The Monpa tribe, inhabiting primarily the western parts of Arunachal Pradesh, predominantly follows Tibetan Buddhism. This is accurate information.

Statement 3 is correct. Arunachal Pradesh is unique among Indian states in that it has a predominantly tribal population, and it officially lacks a Scheduled Caste population. This is a significant demographic characteristic.

All three statements are factually correct.


**4. Consider the following statements regarding the governance of Arunachal Pradesh:**

1. The state is governed by Article 371H of the Indian Constitution, granting special provisions for its administration.
2. The Arunachal Pradesh Legislative Assembly has a minimum strength of 60 members, with a significant number of seats reserved for Scheduled Tribes.
3. The Governor of Arunachal Pradesh holds significant powers in the state's administration, including the power to dissolve the Legislative Assembly.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (c) 1 and 3 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. Article 371H of the Indian Constitution provides special provisions for the administration of Arunachal Pradesh, reflecting the unique challenges and circumstances of the state.

Statement 2 is partially correct but misleading. The Arunachal Pradesh Legislative Assembly has 60 seats, but the number of seats reserved for Scheduled Tribes is not "significant" in the sense of a large majority; almost all seats are reserved for Scheduled Tribes. This is a deliberate attempt to mislead the candidate by using a partially correct fact in a deceptive way.

Statement 3 is correct. The Governor of Arunachal Pradesh, like in other states, holds considerable power in the state's administration, and this includes the power to dissolve the Legislative Assembly under certain constitutional provisions.

Therefore, only statements 1 and 3 are correct.


**5. With reference to Arunachal Pradesh's natural resources, consider the following statements:**

1. Arunachal Pradesh possesses significant reserves of graphite, a crucial mineral used in various industries.
2. The state's forest cover, predominantly consisting of Sub-tropical Moist Pine Forests, contributes significantly to India's carbon stock.
3.  Arunachal Pradesh's tea gardens are primarily located in the Ziro Valley, known for its unique agricultural practices.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (a) 1 and 2 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. Arunachal Pradesh has significant deposits of graphite, a strategically important mineral.

Statement 2 is correct.  The extensive forest cover of Arunachal Pradesh, including Sub-tropical Moist Pine Forests, plays a crucial role in carbon sequestration and contributes to India's overall carbon stock.

Statement 3 is incorrect. While Arunachal Pradesh does have tea gardens, they are not primarily concentrated in the Ziro Valley.  The statement creates a distractor using a true fact (Ziro Valley's presence in Arunachal Pradesh) in an incorrect context.

Therefore, only statements 1 and 2 are correct.


**6. With reference to Manipur's cultural heritage, consider the following statements:**

1. The Sangai, a rare species of deer, is the state animal of Manipur and is endemic to the Loktak Lake.
2.  The Lai Haraoba festival, a significant religious festival, is associated with the worship of deities representing nature.
3. The Manipuri dance form, known for its grace and elegance, is widely practiced across various communities in Manipur and has origins in the Meitei community.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (d) 1, 2, and 3

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. The Sangai deer is indeed the state animal of Manipur and is endemic to the Loktak Lake.

Statement 2 is correct. The Lai Haraoba festival is a significant religious festival deeply intertwined with the worship of deities representing nature and fertility.

Statement 3 is correct. Manipuri dance is a classical dance form primarily associated with the Meitei community but practiced widely across Manipur.

All three statements are factually accurate.


**7. Consider the following statements about Meghalaya's geography and climate:**

1. Meghalaya receives exceptionally high rainfall due to the orographic effect of the Khasi Hills.
2.  The Garo Hills, located in the western part of Meghalaya, are known for their unique dispersed settlements.
3.  The state's forest cover is predominantly composed of Tropical Moist Deciduous Forests, supporting high biodiversity.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (a) 1 and 2 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. The orographic effect caused by the Khasi Hills in Meghalaya leads to exceptionally high rainfall in certain areas, making it one of the wettest regions on Earth.

Statement 2 is correct. The Garo Hills region of Meghalaya is characterized by dispersed settlements, a pattern shaped by the geographical terrain.

Statement 3 is incorrect.  While Meghalaya has significant forest cover and biodiversity, the dominant forest type is not Tropical Moist Deciduous Forests.  The statement misrepresents the actual forest types found in Meghalaya.

Therefore, only statements 1 and 2 are correct.


**8. With reference to Nagaland's socio-cultural landscape, consider the following statements:**

1. The Hornbill Festival, a major tourist attraction, showcases the diverse tribal cultures of Nagaland.
2. The Konyak Naga tribe, inhabiting the easternmost districts, is known for its unique traditions and distinct cultural practices.
3.  The state's official languages include English and Hindi, reflecting its linguistic diversity.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3



**Correct Answer:** (a) 1 and 2 only

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. The Hornbill Festival is a major event promoting Nagaland's rich and diverse tribal cultures.

Statement 2 is correct. The Konyak Naga tribe, inhabiting the eastern parts of Nagaland, is known for its distinct cultural identity and traditions.

Statement 3 is incorrect. While English is an official language of Nagaland, Hindi is not.  This statement introduces a false detail to create a distractor, testing the candidate's knowledge of Nagaland's official languages.

Therefore, only statements 1 and 2 are correct.

**1. Consider the following statements regarding the Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972:**

1.  Schedule I of the Act lists only those species that are critically endangered and face imminent extinction.
2.  The Act prohibits the hunting of all species listed in Schedule II, regardless of any permits or provisions.
3.  The Wildlife Crime Control Bureau was established under the 2006 amendment to the Act.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 1 only
(b) 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. While Schedule I of the Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972, does list highly endangered species, it doesn't exclusively include only those facing imminent extinction.  The criteria for inclusion in Schedule I encompass a broader range of threats and conservation concerns.  Many species are listed due to vulnerability, even if not at the brink of immediate extinction.

Statement 2 is incorrect.  The Act regulates hunting, with Schedule II species requiring special permits and provisions.  Hunting is not categorically prohibited for all Schedule II species. The level of protection varies depending on the species and its status.

Statement 3 is correct. The Wildlife Crime Control Bureau (WCCB) was indeed established through an amendment to the Wildlife (Protection) Act in 2006, to combat wildlife crime more effectively.  This demonstrates the evolution of the Act to address emerging challenges in wildlife conservation.  The establishment of the WCCB highlights the government's commitment to enforcing the Act's provisions and tackling illegal wildlife trade.


**2. With reference to the CITES treaty, consider the following statements:**

1.  Appendix I of CITES lists species that are threatened with extinction and whose international trade is completely prohibited.
2.  Appendix II includes species that are not necessarily threatened but whose trade needs to be carefully monitored to prevent unsustainable exploitation.
3.  India's participation in CITES is solely dependent on its domestic wildlife laws and regulations; CITES has no direct enforcement power within India.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. Appendix I of the Convention on International Trade in Endangered Species of Wild Fauna and Flora (CITES) indeed includes species threatened with extinction, where international commercial trade is generally prohibited, with very limited exceptions.  This reflects the highest level of protection under CITES.

Statement 2 is also correct. Appendix II species are not necessarily threatened with extinction at present, but their trade requires strict monitoring and regulation to prevent overexploitation and ensure their long-term survival.  This level of protection aims to prevent species from reaching a critically endangered status.

Statement 3 is incorrect. While India's domestic laws, like the Wildlife (Protection) Act, are crucial for implementing CITES within its borders, CITES itself does have influence.  India, as a signatory to CITES, is bound by its provisions, and non-compliance can have international repercussions. CITES works through international cooperation and encourages signatory countries to implement the treaty's objectives within their respective jurisdictions.


**3. With reference to the Paris Agreement (2015), consider the following statements:**

1. The Agreement mandates that all member countries achieve net-zero greenhouse gas emissions by 2050.
2. The Agreement sets a target of limiting the global average temperature increase to well below 2°C above pre-industrial levels, pursuing efforts to limit it to 1.5°C.
3. Developed countries pledged to provide $100 billion annually from 2020 to support developing countries in climate mitigation and adaptation, but this commitment has not been consistently met.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 2 and 3 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 1 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect.  The Paris Agreement doesn't mandate a universal net-zero emissions target by 2050 for all countries.  While it encourages the pursuit of net-zero emissions by mid-century, the specific timelines and pathways are determined by individual countries' Nationally Determined Contributions (NDCs).  The Agreement recognizes that different countries have varying capacities and responsibilities.

Statement 2 is correct.  A core objective of the Paris Agreement is to keep the global temperature rise this century well below 2°C above pre-industrial levels and to pursue efforts to limit it to 1.5°C.  This target is based on scientific assessments of the impacts of climate change and underscores the urgency of global action.

Statement 3 is correct. Developed countries did commit to mobilizing $100 billion annually by 2020 to support developing countries' climate actions. However, this commitment has not been fully met, highlighting a significant challenge in achieving the Agreement's goals.  The shortfall underscores the complexities of international climate finance and the need for greater commitment from developed nations.


**4. With reference to the Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs), consider the following statements:**

1.  The SDGs were first proposed in the 1972 Stockholm Declaration on the Human Environment.
2.  The SDGs aim to achieve a set of 17 interconnected global goals by 2030.
3.  The SDGs explicitly include targets for biodiversity conservation and climate change mitigation.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 2 and 3 only
(b) 1 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. While the 1972 Stockholm Declaration laid the groundwork for many environmental initiatives, the Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs) were formally adopted much later, in 2015, as part of the UN's 2030 Agenda for Sustainable Development.  The SDGs build upon, but are distinct from, earlier environmental declarations.

Statement 2 is correct. The SDGs comprise 17 interconnected goals aimed at achieving a more sustainable and equitable future by 2030. These goals address a wide range of issues, from poverty and hunger to health, education, and climate action.

Statement 3 is correct.  The SDGs explicitly include targets related to biodiversity conservation (Goal 15: Life on Land) and climate change mitigation and adaptation (Goal 13: Climate Action).  These goals recognize the interconnectedness of environmental challenges and their impact on sustainable development.


**5. Consider the following statements regarding the National Green Tribunal (NGT):**

1. The NGT has the power to hear cases related to the Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972.
2.  The NGT's orders are binding and can include compensation and damages for environmental damage.
3. The NGT is guided by principles of natural justice but is not bound by the Code of Civil Procedure, 1908.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?
(a) 2 and 3 only
(b) 1 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. The NGT lacks jurisdiction over matters related to the Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972. This is a specific limitation of the NGT's mandate, despite its broad environmental jurisdiction.  Cases under the Wildlife Act typically fall under the purview of other courts and specialized authorities.

Statement 2 is correct. The NGT's orders are indeed binding, and it possesses the authority to award compensation and damages to those affected by environmental violations.  This power is crucial for ensuring accountability and deterring environmentally harmful activities.

Statement 3 is correct. The NGT operates according to the principles of natural justice, ensuring fairness and due process, but it is not bound by the rigid procedures and rules of evidence found in the Code of Civil Procedure, 1908. This allows for a more flexible and efficient approach to environmental dispute resolution.

**1. Consider the following statements regarding the impact of the Kyoto Protocol on different countries:**

1.  India was obligated to meet specific greenhouse gas emission reduction targets under the Kyoto Protocol.
2.  China, as a developing nation, was exempt from mandatory emission reduction targets under the Kyoto Protocol's first commitment period.
3.  The United States' non-ratification of the Kyoto Protocol significantly hampered its effectiveness in achieving global emission reduction goals.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

The Kyoto Protocol, an international treaty under the United Nations Framework Convention on Climate Change (UNFCCC), aimed to reduce greenhouse gas emissions.  A key feature of the protocol was the differentiation between developed and developing countries in terms of emission reduction commitments.  Developed nations, listed in Annex I, were assigned quantified emission limitation and reduction targets (QELROs). Developing nations, not listed in Annex I, were not given such targets initially, recognizing their lower historical contribution to greenhouse gas emissions and their developmental needs.

Statement 1 is incorrect. India, being a developing nation at the time, was not subject to mandatory emission reduction targets under the Kyoto Protocol's first commitment period (2008-2012).  Its participation was focused on adaptation measures and voluntary commitments.

Statement 2 is correct.  China, like India, was not included in Annex I and thus was not bound by the mandatory emission reduction targets during the first commitment period.  The principle of "common but differentiated responsibilities" underpinned this approach.

Statement 3 is correct. The United States, a major emitter of greenhouse gases, notably refused to ratify the Kyoto Protocol. This significantly weakened the protocol's global impact, as the US's participation was crucial for achieving substantial emission reductions.  The absence of the US undermined the treaty's overall effectiveness in addressing climate change.  The lack of participation from major emitters highlighted a significant challenge in achieving international cooperation on environmental issues.


**2. With reference to the 'BioCarbon Fund Initiative for Sustainable Forest Landscapes,' consider the following statements:**

1. The BioCarbon Fund Initiative is primarily managed by the Asian Development Bank, focusing on financing forest conservation projects in Asia.
2.  The initiative provides substantial financial and technical assistance to developing countries for REDD+ (Reducing Emissions from Deforestation and Forest Degradation) efforts.
3.  A major goal of the BioCarbon Fund is to promote sustainable forest management practices, including the development of eco-friendly technologies for timber harvesting.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 2 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

The BioCarbon Fund Initiative for Sustainable Forest Landscapes is a multilateral fund managed by the World Bank. Its primary focus is on providing financial and technical assistance to developing countries to support REDD+ activities.  The fund aims to reduce greenhouse gas emissions from deforestation and forest degradation by creating financial incentives for forest conservation.  The fund does support sustainable forest management but its core mission is REDD+.

Statement 1 is incorrect. The BioCarbon Fund is not managed by the Asian Development Bank. It's managed by the World Bank, with a global scope, not solely focused on Asia.

Statement 2 is correct.  The initiative's core purpose is to provide financial and technical support to developing countries to help them reduce emissions from deforestation and forest degradation.  This support includes capacity building, policy development, and project implementation.

Statement 3 is partially correct, but not the primary focus. While the BioCarbon Fund does indirectly support sustainable forest management by incentivizing reduced deforestation, its emphasis is not directly on developing eco-friendly logging technologies. The focus is on preventing deforestation, not improving logging practices. The fund's objective is to reduce emissions, and sustainable logging is a secondary outcome.




**3. With reference to the 'Global Climate Change Alliance (GCCA),' consider the following statements:**

1.  The GCCA is primarily an initiative of the United Nations Development Programme (UNDP), aimed at assisting developing countries in adapting to climate change.
2. The GCCA facilitates the integration of climate change considerations into national development policies and budgets of participating countries.
3.  The World Bank is the primary coordinating body for the GCCA, providing technical and financial support to the initiative.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) 2 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

The Global Climate Change Alliance (GCCA) is a European Union initiative. Its primary aim is to support developing countries in integrating climate change considerations into their national development policies and budgets. The GCCA provides technical and financial assistance to help these countries implement climate-resilient development strategies.

Statement 1 is incorrect. The GCCA is not primarily an initiative of the UNDP. It is a European Union initiative.

Statement 2 is correct.  A core function of the GCCA is to help countries incorporate climate change into their planning processes. This involves providing technical expertise and funding to support the design and implementation of climate-sensitive policies and programs.

Statement 3 is incorrect. The World Bank is not the coordinating body for the GCCA.  The GCCA is coordinated by the European Commission.


**4. Consider the following statements regarding the 'Arctic Council':**

1.  The Arctic Council is an intergovernmental forum composed solely of Arctic States, focusing on environmental protection and sustainable development in the Arctic region.
2.  Observer status in the Arctic Council is granted exclusively to non-Arctic states that demonstrate significant scientific expertise and commitment to Arctic issues.
3.  The Arctic Council has the authority to enforce binding international agreements related to Arctic resource management and environmental regulations.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) None of the above


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

The Arctic Council is an intergovernmental forum composed of the eight Arctic States: Canada, Denmark (including Greenland and the Faroe Islands), Finland, Iceland, Norway, Russia, Sweden, and the United States.  Its mandate focuses on environmental protection and sustainable development in the Arctic.  The Council works through cooperation among its member states, and also includes observer states and organizations.

Statement 1 is largely correct.  While the council does include observers, its core membership consists of the eight Arctic states.  The focus on environmental protection and sustainable development is accurate.

Statement 2 is incorrect. While observer states must demonstrate a commitment to Arctic issues, scientific expertise is not the sole criterion for acceptance.  The selection process also considers the potential contribution of the observer to the Arctic Council's work.

Statement 3 is incorrect. The Arctic Council is a forum for cooperation, not a regulatory body. It does not have the authority to enforce binding international agreements.  Its recommendations and agreements are non-binding.


**5. With reference to the 'Global Alliance for Climate-Smart Agriculture (GACSA),' consider the following statements:**

1.  GACSA was established as a direct outcome of the 2015 Paris Agreement on climate change.
2.  Participation in GACSA entails legally binding commitments for member countries to adopt specific climate-smart agricultural practices.
3.  The Food and Agriculture Organization of the United Nations (FAO) plays a significant role in promoting and coordinating the activities of GACSA.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

The Global Alliance for Climate-Smart Agriculture (GACSA) is a voluntary partnership.  While it emerged from discussions surrounding climate change and agriculture, it is not a direct outcome of the Paris Agreement.  Membership does not create legally binding obligations.  The FAO plays a significant role in its promotion and coordination.

Statement 1 is incorrect.  GACSA was not directly established by the Paris Agreement. It is a separate initiative aimed at promoting climate-smart agriculture.

Statement 2 is incorrect. GACSA is a voluntary alliance. There are no binding commitments for its members. Participation is based on shared goals and collaborative efforts.

Statement 3 is correct. The FAO is a key partner in GACSA, actively involved in promoting its principles and facilitating collaboration among its members.  The FAO's expertise in agriculture and its global reach contribute significantly to GACSA's work.

Here are some UPSC-style multiple choice questions based on the provided target content, adhering to all specified criteria.  Each question includes the correct answer and a detailed explanation.


**1. Consider the following statements regarding poverty reduction strategies:**

1.  The implementation of inclusive growth policies consistently leads to a significant reduction in poverty levels across all socioeconomic groups.
2.  Economic growth, irrespective of its distributional impact, invariably translates into a proportionate decrease in poverty.
3.  Remittances from overseas workers always contribute positively to poverty reduction in their home countries, regardless of the recipient's economic status or the country's economic policies.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

None of the statements are entirely correct.  Statement 1 is incorrect because inclusive growth, while aiming to reduce poverty, doesn't guarantee its elimination across all groups.  The effectiveness depends on the design and implementation of the policies, and certain segments of the population may still be marginalized. Statement 2 is flawed because economic growth alone is insufficient for poverty reduction. If the benefits of growth are not equitably distributed, poverty may persist, or even worsen, for certain segments.  Statement 3 is false because while remittances can contribute to poverty reduction, their impact is contingent on several factors, including how the money is used, the recipient's financial literacy, and the overall economic situation of the receiving household and country.  Effective poverty reduction necessitates a multifaceted approach combining economic growth with equitable distribution, social safety nets, and targeted interventions.


**2. With reference to the impact of economic policies on poverty reduction, consider the following statements:**

1.  The 1991 economic reforms in India directly resulted in a rapid and uniform decline in poverty across all states.
2.  Socialist economic policies, historically implemented in several countries, have consistently proven highly effective in eradicating poverty.
3.  Agricultural growth is a crucial factor in poverty reduction, particularly in agrarian economies, but its effectiveness varies based on factors like land distribution and access to markets.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 3 only
(c) 1 only
(d) 2 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Only statement 3 is correct. The 1991 reforms in India led to economic growth, but poverty reduction was uneven across states, influenced by factors like regional disparities and access to opportunities.  Statement 2 is incorrect; socialist policies have had mixed results in poverty reduction, with some showing limited success and others leading to economic stagnation and persistent poverty. Statement 3 accurately reflects the importance of agricultural growth in poverty reduction, especially in countries with large agrarian populations. However, the impact is conditional; equitable land distribution and access to markets are crucial for the benefits to reach the poorest.


**3. With reference to the Greenhouse Gas Protocol, consider the following statements:**

1.  The Greenhouse Gas Protocol is primarily a legally binding international treaty that sets mandatory emission reduction targets for all participating nations.
2.  The protocol’s framework focuses solely on providing financial incentives to developing countries to adopt cleaner technologies.
3.  It offers a standardized accounting and reporting framework for businesses and governments to measure and manage their greenhouse gas emissions.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) 1 and 2 only


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Only statement 3 is correct. The Greenhouse Gas Protocol is not a legally binding treaty; it's a voluntary initiative providing a widely accepted accounting standard for greenhouse gas emissions.  It doesn't mandate specific emission reduction targets or solely focus on financial incentives for developing countries.  Instead, it provides a framework for companies and governments to measure, report, and manage their emissions, contributing to a more transparent and comparable understanding of the global greenhouse gas situation.  This allows for better informed decision-making regarding climate change mitigation.


**4. Consider the following statements about Agenda 21:**

1.  Agenda 21 was primarily developed during the World Summit on Sustainable Development in Johannesburg in 2002.
2.  The document focuses exclusively on environmental issues, neglecting the social and economic dimensions of sustainable development.
3.  It is a comprehensive action plan for sustainable development, encompassing environmental protection, social equity, and economic growth.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) 1 and 2 only


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Only statement 3 is correct. Agenda 21 originated from the Earth Summit in Rio de Janeiro in 1992, not the Johannesburg summit in 2002.  Furthermore, Agenda 21 is not solely focused on environmental issues; it's a holistic plan addressing social and economic aspects of sustainable development.  It aims to integrate environmental considerations into economic and social policies, promoting a balanced approach to development that considers the needs of present and future generations.


**5. With reference to the components of the Air Quality Index (AQI) in Indian cities, consider the following statements:**

1.  Methane is a primary component considered in calculating the AQI.
2.  Carbon dioxide is a key pollutant included in the AQI calculation.
3.  Nitrogen dioxide, sulfur dioxide, and carbon monoxide are all included in the AQI.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 3 only
(c) 2 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Only statement 3 is correct.  The AQI in Indian cities typically includes nitrogen dioxide, sulfur dioxide, and carbon monoxide as major pollutants. Methane and carbon dioxide are greenhouse gases, but their inclusion in the AQI is not standard, primarily because they are less directly related to immediate health impacts compared to the other pollutants. The AQI focuses on pollutants with short-term health effects, while greenhouse gases have longer-term climatic effects.


**6. With reference to the Green India Mission's aims, consider the following statements:**

1.  The Green India Mission's primary goal is to implement "green accounting" by incorporating environmental costs and benefits into national budgets.
2.  A key objective is to launch a second green revolution, focused on enhancing agricultural output to ensure future food security.
3.  The mission aims to restore and enhance forest cover as a strategy for climate change mitigation and adaptation.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) 1 and 2 only


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Only statement 3 accurately reflects a core aim of the Green India Mission.  While green accounting is a relevant concept for environmental policy, it's not the primary focus of the Green India Mission. The mission does not primarily aim to launch a second green revolution; its focus is on ecological restoration and environmental sustainability.  The mission's key objective is to increase forest cover and biodiversity to enhance carbon sequestration, improve water resources, and promote climate resilience.


**7.  Consider the following statements regarding unique features of National Parks in India:**

1.  Keibul Lamjao National Park is distinctive for its swampy terrain and floating vegetation supporting rich biodiversity.
2.  Bhitarkanika National Park is known for its high-altitude climate, ranging from tropical to arctic conditions.
3.  Khangchendzonga National Park is characterized by its diverse climate zones, encompassing tropical, subtropical, temperate, and arctic regions.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) 1 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

Statements 1 and 3 are correct. Keibul Lamjao National Park, located on Loktak Lake, is indeed unique for its floating vegetation and swamp ecosystem supporting a diverse range of flora and fauna. Khangchendzonga National Park, situated in the Himalayas, exhibits a wide range of climatic zones, from tropical at lower altitudes to arctic conditions at higher elevations. Statement 2 is incorrect; Bhitarkanika is a coastal wetland, not a high-altitude park with an arctic climate.  The diverse climatic zones are a key characteristic of Khangchendzonga, not Bhitarkanika.


**8. With reference to the Green Climate Fund (GCF), consider the following statements:**

1.  The GCF is primarily intended to assist developed countries in adopting mitigation and adaptation strategies to counter climate change.
2.  It is established under the auspices of the United Nations Environment Programme (UNEP).
3.  The GCF primarily supports developing countries in their adaptation and mitigation efforts to address climate change.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) 1 and 2 only


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Only statement 3 is correct. The Green Climate Fund is designed to support developing countries, not developed nations, in their efforts to mitigate and adapt to climate change. The GCF is established under the UNFCCC (United Nations Framework Convention on Climate Change), not UNEP.  The GCF's primary mandate is to provide financial resources to assist vulnerable countries in implementing climate-resilient development strategies.  The fund plays a crucial role in achieving global climate goals by channeling financial resources to where they are most needed.

**1. Consider the following statements regarding the Khangchendzonga National Park:**

1.  It is located in the state of Arunachal Pradesh and is primarily known for its diverse flora and fauna.
2.  The park's UNESCO World Heritage Site status is primarily attributed to its significant cultural heritage, specifically its association with Buddhism.
3.  The park's conservation efforts are solely focused on preserving its unique biodiversity and have minimal integration with local communities.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. Khangchendzonga National Park is situated in Sikkim, not Arunachal Pradesh.  While the park boasts rich biodiversity, its UNESCO World Heritage status recognizes a broader scope encompassing its ecological and cultural significance.

Statement 2 is correct. Khangchendzonga National Park's inscription as a UNESCO World Heritage Site highlights its mixed natural and cultural heritage.  The area holds deep spiritual and cultural significance for local communities, particularly those practicing Buddhism, who consider the mountain sacred. This cultural dimension is a key aspect of its recognition.

Statement 3 is incorrect. The park's management actively involves local communities in conservation efforts, recognizing their traditional knowledge and the importance of their sustainable livelihoods in preserving the park's integrity.  A community-based approach is crucial for the long-term success of conservation initiatives.  The UNESCO criteria for World Heritage sites often emphasize the importance of involving local communities in the management and protection of such sites.


**2. With reference to the Green Climate Fund, consider the following statements:**

1. The Green Climate Fund primarily focuses on assisting developed nations in adapting to the impacts of climate change.
2. The fund operates independently from the United Nations Framework Convention on Climate Change (UNFCCC).
3.  The World Bank is one of the entities involved in managing the Green Climate Fund.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. The Green Climate Fund's core mandate is to support developing countries in mitigation and adaptation measures to address climate change. It prioritizes assisting vulnerable nations in reducing greenhouse gas emissions and building resilience to climate impacts.

Statement 2 is incorrect. The Green Climate Fund is established under the UNFCCC to support its goals. It serves as a financial mechanism for the convention, channeling funds towards climate action in developing countries.  Its operations are closely aligned with the UNFCCC's objectives and reporting frameworks.

Statement 3 is correct. The World Bank is one of several accredited entities that can receive funding from the Green Climate Fund and manage projects on its behalf.  It plays a role in the fund's operational framework, although it does not solely manage the fund. Other international organizations and national implementing entities also participate in the fund's activities.


**3. With reference to BirdLife International, consider the following statements:**

1. BirdLife International is primarily a governmental organization focused on bird conservation within specific national jurisdictions.
2. The concept of "biodiversity hotspots" originated from the World Wildlife Fund (WWF), not BirdLife International.
3. BirdLife International's designation of Important Bird and Biodiversity Areas (IBAs) is solely based on the presence of endangered bird species.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. BirdLife International is a global partnership of conservation organizations, not a governmental entity. Its work spans numerous countries, collaborating with a wide network of partners to protect birds and biodiversity globally.

Statement 2 is correct.  While BirdLife International plays a significant role in biodiversity conservation, the concept of "biodiversity hotspots" originated from Conservation International (CI), not the World Wildlife Fund (WWF) or BirdLife International.  CI identified these areas based on high levels of endemic species and significant habitat loss.

Statement 3 is incorrect. BirdLife International's IBA designation considers a broader range of factors beyond just endangered bird species.  IBAs are identified based on the presence of globally significant bird populations, including those that are not necessarily endangered, and also taking into account other biodiversity values within the area. The selection criteria for IBAs are comprehensive and include factors such as representation of threatened species, biome representation, and concentrations of restricted-range species.


**4. With reference to the Forest Carbon Partnership Facility (FCPF), consider the following statements:**

1. The FCPF primarily provides funding to universities for research into sustainable forestry practices.
2.  The FCPF is solely managed by the Asian Development Bank.
3. The FCPF's support for REDD+ efforts is limited to providing technical assistance, not financial aid.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. While the FCPF may support some research indirectly through its projects, its primary focus is not direct funding to universities. The FCPF's core activities are centered on supporting developing countries in reducing emissions from deforestation and forest degradation (REDD+).

Statement 2 is incorrect. The FCPF is managed by the World Bank, not the Asian Development Bank.  The World Bank acts as the trustee and secretariat of the FCPF, overseeing its operations and coordinating its activities with partner countries and organizations.

Statement 3 is incorrect. The FCPF provides both financial and technical assistance to countries involved in REDD+ efforts. Financial support is a crucial element of the FCPF's strategy for incentivizing sustainable forest management and reducing deforestation.  The technical assistance component is also vital, providing guidance and capacity building to countries implementing REDD+ programs.


**5. With reference to the Genetic Engineering Appraisal Committee (GEAC), consider the following statements:**

1. The GEAC is constituted under the Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972.
2. The GEAC's primary function is to assess the environmental impact of genetically modified organisms (GMOs).
3. The GEAC's decisions are not legally binding and are purely advisory in nature.

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. The GEAC is constituted under the Environment (Protection) Act, 1986, not the Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972.  Its mandate is to regulate activities related to genetic engineering, including the release of GMOs into the environment.

Statement 2 is correct. The GEAC's core function involves appraising the environmental implications of genetically modified organisms and related technologies. It assesses the potential risks and benefits of such technologies before they are released into the environment. Its role is crucial for safeguarding environmental safety.

Statement 3 is incorrect. The GEAC's decisions are legally binding.  Its approvals or rejections of proposals relating to genetic engineering are crucial regulatory steps that must be followed by applicants.  Non-compliance can have legal ramifications.  The GEAC's authority stems from the Environment (Protection) Act, 1986, which grants the central government the power to regulate activities that may have adverse environmental consequences.



**6. With reference to the Montreux Record, consider the following statements:**

1.  The Montreux Record only lists wetlands located in developed countries.
2. Inclusion of a wetland in the Montreux Record necessitates the immediate cessation of all human activities within the wetland.
3.  The Montreux Record is maintained by the Convention on Biological Diversity (CBD).

Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. The Montreux Record includes wetlands of international importance from both developed and developing countries.  It focuses on wetlands listed under the Ramsar Convention, irrespective of the economic status of the country where they are located.

Statement 2 is incorrect.  Inclusion in the Montreux Record signifies that changes in a wetland's ecological character have occurred or are likely to occur due to human interference.  It does not automatically mandate the immediate halt of all human activities.  Rather, it highlights the need for careful monitoring, management intervention, and possibly remedial action to restore the wetland's ecological integrity.  The aim is to address the negative impacts of human activities, not necessarily to completely halt all such activities.

Statement 3 is incorrect. The Montreux Record is maintained by the Ramsar Convention on Wetlands, not the Convention on Biological Diversity (CBD).  The Ramsar Convention is a specific international treaty focused on the conservation and wise use of wetlands.  The Montreux Record serves as a mechanism within the Ramsar framework to highlight wetlands that require special attention due to ecological changes.

Here are some UPSC-style multiple-choice questions based on the provided target content, adhering to all specified criteria.  Each question includes the correct answer and a detailed explanation.


**1. Consider the following statements regarding the Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972:**

1.  The Act mandates the creation of a Wildlife Advisory Board at the national level, responsible for advising the government on wildlife conservation strategies.
2.  Schedule VI of the Act regulates the trade and cultivation of all plant species found within India's geographical boundaries, regardless of their conservation status.
3.  The Act explicitly grants the National Green Tribunal (NGT) jurisdiction over all matters pertaining to the enforcement of its provisions.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is correct. The Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972, indeed mandates the establishment of a Wildlife Advisory Board to provide expert advice to the government on wildlife-related matters. This board plays a crucial role in policy formulation and implementation.

Statement 2 is incorrect. While Schedule VI of the Act does regulate the trade and cultivation of certain plant species, it doesn't encompass *all* plant species in India.  The scope is limited to specific plants mentioned in the schedule, primarily focusing on those with conservation concerns or potential for illegal trade.

Statement 3 is incorrect. The National Green Tribunal (NGT) does not have jurisdiction over matters related to the Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972.  This is a significant point to remember as it highlights the division of environmental jurisdiction between different legal bodies in India.  The enforcement of the Wildlife Act primarily falls under the purview of state and central forest departments.



**2. With reference to the schedules within the Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972, consider the following statements:**

1. Schedule I lists only those species considered to be of least concern according to IUCN Red List criteria.
2. Schedule II provides a list of species whose hunting is strictly prohibited, while Schedule III regulates the hunting of certain game species.
3. Schedule V includes species deemed to be vermin and whose hunting is permitted under specific conditions.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) 2 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. Schedule I of the Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972, lists the most endangered and critically threatened species, offering them the highest level of protection.  These are not species of "least concern".

Statement 2 is correct. Schedule II indeed lists species with absolute hunting prohibitions, while Schedule III regulates the hunting of certain game animals, often with licensing requirements and restrictions.  This highlights the tiered approach to species protection under the Act.

Statement 3 is correct. Schedule V lists animals classified as vermin, whose hunting is permitted under specific conditions and with certain regulations.  This addresses the need to manage populations of certain species that might pose agricultural or other challenges.



**3. With reference to Eco-Sensitive Zones (ESZs) in India, consider the following statements:**

1.  The declaration of ESZs is solely based on the provisions outlined in the Environment (Protection) Act, 1986, and excludes any reference to the Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972.
2.  The primary objective of declaring ESZs is to completely prohibit all human activities within the designated area, irrespective of their sustainability or impact.
3.  Agriculture, specifically organic farming, is generally permitted within ESZs, while other activities are subject to varying degrees of regulation and restriction.


Which of the statements given above is/are correct?

(a) 1 only
(b) 3 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Statement 1 is incorrect. While the Environment (Protection) Act, 1986, provides the legal framework for declaring ESZs, the concept often arises from the need to protect areas surrounding national parks and wildlife sanctuaries, thus implicitly linking it to the Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972.  The proximity of ESZs to protected areas underscores the interconnectedness of environmental legislation.

Statement 2 is incorrect. The purpose of ESZs is not to completely ban all human activities.
